# Project Status

## Overall Progress

Reset on extraction (`archon extract`) from the Algebraic-Jacobian challenge.

This subproject's scope is the ƒåech computation of higher direct images
(`AlgebraicGeometry.cech_computes_higherDirectImage`, `lem:cech_computes_cohomology`)
and its 12-node dependency cone. See `PROGRESS.md` for the open-obligation inventory and
`STRATEGY.md` for the proof arc. The parent project's prover-execution history and
knowledge base were left behind with the carved-away material; this file will be
repopulated by this subproject's own review phase.

## Knowledge Base

- **MODULE-SHEAF iso-by-reflection + the `toPresheaf ‚ãô evaluation` INSTANCE TRAP (iter-061, `isIso_modules_of_toPresheaf` + `isIso_prodLift_of_isLimit` + `coprodDecompMap` axiom-clean; `isIso_coprodDecompMap` BLOCKED on the trap)**: foundations for the CSI Stub-2 disjoint-union chain. The standard cover is of a **proper** `D(f)`, so `Ideal.span (range g) = ‚ä§` FAILS (only `f`-units are covered). The Stacks 02KG "Write `U = Spec(A)`" fix is **change of base to `R_f = Localization.Away f`**: each `Œì(D(gœÉ),~_R M) = M[1/gœÉ]` is already an `R_f`-module, and over `R_f` the family `{g·µ¢/1}` DOES span `‚ä§` (the closed leaf `affine_cover_span_localizationAway`: `‚Üê iSup_basicOpen_eq_top_iff`, `simp [‚Üê comap_basicOpen]`, `map_iSup`, `‚Üê hcov`, `comap_basicOpen`, `D(unit)=‚ä§` via `IsLocalization.Away.algebraMap_isUnit` + `Ideal.eq_top_of_isUnit_mem`). The HEAVY residual leaf (`htilde`, multi-session, comparable to the keystone chain) is a **change-of-space iso of section ƒåech COCHAIN complexes** `sectionCechComplex (D_R g)(~_R M) ‚âÖ sectionCechComplex (D_{R_f} g/1)(~_{R_f} M_f)` ‚Äî the `CechAcyclic` module machinery (`sectionToModuleAddEquiv`/`dDiff_exact`/`phi`/`dCoeff`) is `private` so an `R_f`-direct re-derivation is unavailable; the public `sectionCech_affine_vanishing` forces the change-of-space route. **`Ext` performance:** any file using `Ext` over `(Spec R).Modules` must `attribute [local instance] hasExtModules` (the `HasExt.standard` from `AbsoluteCohomology.lean`) AND spell `CategoryTheory.Abelian.Ext` fully-qualified ‚Äî both dodge the slow `HasSmallLocalizedHom`/overload typeclass timeout (20000-heartbeat). Reductions threaded as explicit `htilde` hypothesis (no sorry); axiom-clean.
- **01I8 CLOSED ‚Äî the tilde‚ÄìŒì counit is an iso for qcoh `F`; `qcoh_iso_tilde_sections` now UNCONDITIONAL (iter-048, `isIso_fromTildeŒì_of_quasicoherent`, the LAST 01I8 step)**:
  the Route B section-localization program (iters 040‚Üí048) is complete. Recipe to prove a `TopCat.Sheaf (ModuleCat R)` morphism is an iso by checking it on the basis of distinguished opens `{D(r)}`:
  (1) `suffices h : IsIso (modulesSpecToSheaf.map F.fromTildeŒì) from SpecModulesToSheafFullyFaithful.isIso_of_isIso_map F.fromTildeŒì` ‚Äî reflect through the fully faithful forget; the `suffices ‚Ä¶ from` form is MANDATORY to defer the eager synthesis of the `[IsIso (F.map f)]` argument that a direct `apply` triggers (`failed to synthesize`).
  (2) `Functor.IsCoverDense.iso_of_restrict_iso` over `inducedFunctor (fun r => specBasicOpen r)`, cover-dense via `TopCat.Opens.coverDense_inducedFunctor PrimeSpectrum.isBasis_basic_opens` (`IsLocallyFull` auto from `IsLocallyFull.of_full`).

  **GOTCHAS (each cost a debugging round):** `TopCat.Sheaf` morphisms project the underlying NatTrans via `.hom`, NOT `.val`/`.1` (they are `InducedCategory.Hom`). Whisker via `G.op.whiskerLeft` (= `Functor.whiskerLeft`); bare `whiskerLeft` out of scope. The basis functor MUST land in `(Spec R).Opens` ‚Äî use project abbrev `specBasicOpen`, NOT bare `PrimeSpectrum.basicOpen` (else `‚Üë?X =?= PrimeSpectrum R` space-unification fails against the Grothendieck topology). The per-`D(r)` component is iso because `c.hom ‚àò‚Çó tilde.toOpen.hom = œÅ_r` (Mathlib `Scheme.Modules.toOpen_fromTildeŒì_app`, read at `.hom`/LinearMap via `congrArg ModuleCat.Hom.hom` + `ModuleCat.hom_comp`); both `tilde.toOpen.hom` (Mathlib instance) and `œÅ_r` (keystone `qcoh_section_isLocalizedModule`) are `IsLocalizedModule (powers r)` of `Œì(X,F)`, so `c.hom = IsLocalizedModule.linearEquiv ‚Ä¶` (via `IsLocalizedModule.ext` + `map_units`), bijective ‚üπ iso by `ConcreteCategory.isIso_iff_bijective`. **`IsLocalizedModule.linearEquiv_of_isLocalizedModule_comp` does NOT exist** (loogle false positive) ‚Äî use `linearEquiv` + `ext`. Kernel-verified ({propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}). `analogies` / memory: `sheaf-iso-on-basis-plumbing`.

Thin-cat morphism equalities close via `congrArg (‚Ä¶ map m ‚Ä¶) (Subsingleton.elim _ _)` (the SAFE form, NOT the spurious-rfl trap ‚Äî lean-auditor confirmed). `overlap_target_eq` (`D((a¬∑b)¬∑f)=D(af)‚äìD(bf)`) needs explicit `le_antisymm` (8 `inf_le_*` chains), NOT `inf_inf_inf_comm`/`inf_idem`. The `IsLocalizedModule.iso`/`.lift` instance on a `homOfLE`-laden diamond map must be `@`-THREADED, not `haveI`/`letI` (TC search fails). Under `maxHeartbeats 1000000`. Kernel-verified ({propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}). The next-iter `fromTildeŒì` assembly WILL hit this same diamond ‚Äî apply this recipe.
- **W1/W2/W3 DISSOLVED ‚Äî ROUTE THE BASE-RING DESCENT THROUGH THE BUNDLED `restrictScalars` CARRIER (iter-046, `tile_section_localization` BUILT axiom-clean, the LAST keystone leaf, 01I8)**:

  `LinearMap.ext; simp [reconcile applies]; exact tile_restrict_map_apply ‚Ä¶`;

  `keyB` closed at the uniform `ModuleCat.Hom.hom` level: `rw [‚Üê ModuleCat.hom_comp, ‚Üê Functor.map_comp]; exact congrArg (F.presheaf.map ¬∑).hom (Subsingleton.elim _ _)`.

  (`lake env lean` exit 0; `#print axioms` = {propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound}).
- **`Spec`-DEPENDENT INSTANCES MUST BE PASSED INLINE, NEVER `letI`/`haveI`/`have` (iter-045, `tile_section_localization` assembly, 01I8 keystone) [SUPERSEDED by the restrictScalars-carrier recipe above ‚Äî the wall this describes is no longer hit]**:
  inside a `lemma`/`theorem`, introducing ANY instance whose definition mentions `Spec` (a `Module R` on a

  instance passed by `@`-position so earlier positions feed later ones; build `IsScalarTower` via

- **`sync_leanok` IS FOOLED BY A COMMENTED-OUT `lemma <name>` IN THE `.lean` FILE (iter-045, DAG-poisoning)**:
  a commented-out sketch `/- ‚Ä¶ lemma tile_section_localization ‚Ä¶ -/` in the source caused `sync_leanok` to add/keep
  `\leanok` on the blueprint block `lem:tile_section_localization` even though the real decl does NOT exist
  (the analyzer keys off `\lean{}` + a sorry-scan that the commented `lemma` text satisfies). This falsely marks
  the block ‚Äî and its whole downstream cone ‚Äî as proved in the dependency graph. Mitigation: do NOT leave a
  commented-out `lemma <exact-blueprint-target-name>` in the source; rename/mangle the sketch
  (e.g. `‚Ä¶_SKETCH`, or wrap as ```` ```text ````). Review can override the false `\leanok` (authorized when certain),
  but it re-appears next sync until the source sketch is mangled.

  the iter-034 germ-naturality helper `tilde_stalkFunctor_map_toStalk` (insert `LinearMap.comp_apply` before `map_apply`).
- **Presentation transport across a slice‚Üîsubspace site equivalence (iter-037, `presentationOverBasicOpen`, 01I8 Route B B2)**:
  to restrict a presentation of `M.over U` to `M.over D(g)` when `D(g) ‚äÜ U`, mirror Mathlib
  `SheafOfModules.QuasicoherentData.bind`'s presentation field. With `W := Over.mk (homOfLE hg) : Over U` (so
  `W.left = specBasicOpen g`), build `e := pushforwardPushforwardEquivalence (Over.iteratedSliceEquiv W) (ùüô _) (ùüô _) ‚Ä¶`
  (ring-sheaf compat is `R.1.map_id` here because both ring sheaves are `‚Ä¶over` of the same base), then
  `P.map (pushforward (ùüô _))` ‚Üí `.map e.inverse` ‚Üí `Presentation.ofIsIso` along the counit-preimage iso.
  **Five elaboration traps (REUSE for B3/B4):** (1) write the equiv-codomain ring sheaf with `W.left` LITERALLY
  (`(R := (Spec R).ringCatSheaf.over W.left)`), not the reduced `specBasicOpen g` ‚Äî the
  `Over.iteratedSliceForward.IsContinuous ‚Ä¶ (J.over f.left)` instance matches on `f.left` syntactically;
  (2) pin `Presentation.ofIsIso.{u,u,u}` (else `[HasSheafify (J.over ‚Ä¶)]` resolves `AddCommGrpCat.{0}` ‚Üí
  `Type 1` vs `Type (u+1)`); (3) give the counit iso an explicit `letI iso : e.inverse.obj (‚Ä¶) ‚âÖ M.over W.left :=
  e.fullyFaithfulFunctor.preimageIso (by exact e.counitIso.app (‚Ä¶))`; (4) `set_option
  backward.isDefEq.respectTransparency false in` before the def (bridges `e.functor.obj (M.over W.left) =?=
  (M.over U).over W`, only visible at all-transparency); (5) `show (M.over W.left).Presentation from ‚Ä¶` to bridge
  to the declared return type. NOTE for B3: there the two ring sheaves are GENUINELY different (over-ring-sheaf on
  `Over D(g)` vs subscheme structure sheaf on `Opens ‚Ü•D(g)`), so the compat datum is built from the open-immersion
  `(specBasicOpen g).Œπ.appIso` ‚Äî real geometric content, NOT `map_id`.
- **Closing a site-equivalence continuity TODO (iter-037, `Opens.overEquivalence_{functor,inverse}_isContinuous`, 01I8 Route B)**:
  Mathlib's `TopologicalSpace.Opens.overEquivalence U : Over U ‚âå Opens ‚Ü•U` exists but its `## TODO` leaves both
  functors' continuity unproven (needed to instantiate `pushforwardPushforwardEquivalence` on this site equivalence).

  predicate, `GrothendieckTopology.mem_over_iff` unfolds the over-topology, `‚ü®x', hx'U‚ü©`/`Subtype.val` bookkeeping),

  `IsLocallyFaithful` auto-derive from the equivalence-of-sites instances. `CompatiblePreserving` is NOT involved
  (a stale-docstring trap ‚Äî the real drivers are `IsLocallyFull`+`IsLocallyFaithful`).
- **restrict‚Üîover module equivalence via `pushforwardPushforwardEquivalence` (iter-038, `modulesOverBasicOpenEquivalence`, 01I8 Route B B3b)**:
  to bridge `(specBasicOpen g).toScheme.Modules ‚âå SheafOfModules ((Spec R).ringCatSheaf.over D(g))`,
  feed `pushforwardPushforwardEquivalence (Opens.overEquivalence (specBasicOpen g)) œÜ œà H‚ÇÅ H‚ÇÇ`. Key:
  `Scheme.Opens.Œπ_appIso = Iso.refl` (Mathlib `Restrict.lean:98`) ‚üπ the open-immersion structure-sheaf
  comparison is the identity, and `toScheme_presheaf_obj/_map` are `rfl` ‚üπ both ring sheaves factor
  through `(Spec R).ringCatSheaf.val` definitionally, so œÜ/œà are just whiskerings of `overForgetIso.inv`
  / `overForgetInvIso.inv` (the latter `= Iso.refl`). `overForgetIso : Over.forget D(g) ‚âÖ
  overEquivalence.functor ‚ãô Œπ.opensFunctor` has automatic naturality (thin `Opens`), object component
  `eqToIso` of the image‚Äìpreimage identity `Œπ ''·µÅ (Œπ‚Åª¬π·µÅ V) = V` (proved `Set.image_preimage_eq_of_subset
  (fun x hx => ‚ü®‚ü®x, leOfHom V.hom hx‚ü©, rfl‚ü©)`). Continuity instances must be re-stated for the `toScheme`
  carrier (`‚Ü•D(g).toScheme`, defeq-not-syntactic to `‚Ü•D(g)`) so instance search fires. H‚ÇÅ component index
  is `(Opens ‚Ü•D(g))·µí·µñ`, H‚ÇÇ is `(Over D(g))·µí·µñ` ‚Äî do NOT mix.
- **B3 object iso + B4 presentation transport (iter-040, `overBasicOpenIsoRestrict` / `presentationModulesRestrictBasicOpen`, 01I8 Route B B3c/B4)**:
  the assembled bridge `(modulesOverBasicOpenEquivalence g).inverse.obj (M.over D(g)) ‚âÖ M.restrict Œπ` is
  `(pushforwardComp (overBasicOpenRingInvHom g) (ùüô _)).app M ‚â™‚â´ (pushforwardCongr h).app M`. Three
  reusable elaboration idioms surfaced (all verified kernel-clean, `#print axioms` = the 3 standard
  axioms): (1) **discrimination-tree IsContinuous mismatch on `.toScheme` sites** ‚Äî `pushforwardComp`
  wants `IsContinuous` of the inverse + composite in the `‚Ü•‚Üë(specBasicOpen g)`/`TopCat.str`-coercion form,
  which does NOT match the file's `.toScheme` instances; fix = `set_option
  backward.isDefEq.respectTransparency false in` on the def (unifies `TopCat.str` with
  `SheafedSpace.instTopologicalSpaceCarrierCarrier`) + local `haveI`s
  (`overEquivalence_inverse_isContinuous_toScheme`, `Functor.isContinuous_comp`), and pin
  `G := Over.forget ‚Ä¶`/`R' := ‚Ä¶` on `pushforwardComp` or `G` stays a stuck metavar. This option is
  **elaborator-only and kernel-safe** (kernel re-checks independently ‚Äî confirmed by lean-auditor).
  (2) the residual `pushforwardCongr` data equality closes by `ext U : 3; simp [overBasicOpenRingInvHom,
  overForgetInvIso, Scheme.Opens.Œπ_appIso]; rfl` ‚Äî both sides reduce to `forget‚ÇÇ.map ùüô` on defeq opens;
  this is a GENUINE definitional rfl, NOT the thin-category spurious-rfl trap (lean-auditor verified the
  pre-`rfl` goal). (3) **inline instance search drops exact-type local `PreservesColimitsOfSize` / `IsIso`**
  (universe-form mismatch): build the instance as a local `haveI hpc := inferInstance` and `@`-apply the
  consumer with it explicit (`@SheafOfModules.Presentation.map ‚Ä¶ hpc ‚Ä¶`, `@asIso _ _ _ _ _ inst`), pinning
  functor universes (`restrictFunctor.{u}`); also `Presentation.ofIsIso.{u,u,u}` must pin universes (defaults
  to 0); raise `synthInstance.maxHeartbeats 400000` for the localized-site colimit search. B4 chains
  B2 over-presentation ‚Üí `.map engine.inverse` ‚Üí `ofIsIso` (B3 bridge) ‚Üí `.map (restrictFunctor ‚Ä¶)` with
  unit-iso `restrictBasicOpenUnitIso` (= `restrictFunctorIsoPullback ‚â™‚â´ asIso pullbackObjUnitToUnit`,
  iso because the affine `Opens.map` is final via `Opens.mapMapIso (asIso ‚Ä¶base) |>.isEquivalence_functor`).
- **Thin-category coherence kernel-soundness trap ‚Äî `ext`/`congr 1` produce kernel-rejected terms (iter-038, CRITICAL)**:
  when closing a thin-category coherence square (H‚ÇÅ/H‚ÇÇ-style, over `Opens`/`Over (Opens X)`) by morphism
  uniqueness, a bare `ext (V : ‚Ä¶)` or `congr 1` can **auto-close the goal with an unsound term the LSP
  ACCEPTS but `lake env lean` REJECTS** with `error: unknown free variable _fvar‚Ä¶`. The LSP showed
  "solved"; only the kernel caught it. FIX: write the proof as an explicit term ‚Äî `refine NatTrans.ext
  (funext fun V => ?_); simp only [‚Ä¶]; erw [‚Üê Functor.map_comp]; exact congrArg P.val.map
  (Subsingleton.elim _ _)` (H‚ÇÇ adds `.trans (P.map_id _)`). The `Subsingleton.elim` on morphisms is the
  genuine, non-vacuous proof (`Opens`/`Over (Opens X)` are thin). ALWAYS confirm coherence/defeq-heavy
  proofs with `lake env lean` + `#print axioms`, NEVER trust the LSP's "no goals" alone.
- **`(Spec R).Opens` defeq impedance (iter-032, `standard_cover_cofinal`)**: the carrier of `(Spec R).Opens` is
  `‚Ü•(Spec R)`, defeq but not syntactically equal to `PrimeSpectrum ‚ÜëR`. Coercing a *variable* `Uf : (Spec R).Opens`
  to `Set ‚Ü•(Spec R)` works; coercing an inline ascription `(PrimeSpectrum.basicOpen r : (Spec R).Opens)` to
  `Set ‚Ü•(Spec R)` does NOT (the SetLike coercion is not inserted, giving "type mismatch ‚Ä¶ Opens (PrimeSpectrum ‚ÜëR)
  vs Set ‚Ü•(Spec R)"). FIX: bind first via `set Uf : (Spec R).Opens := PrimeSpectrum.basicOpen f` and
  `let B : R ‚Üí (Spec R).Opens := fun r => PrimeSpectrum.basicOpen r`, then coerce `Uf`/`B r`. Use `change` not
  `show` (dodges the show-tactic linter). Cofinal-refinement skeleton: `PrimeSpectrum.isCompact_basicOpen` +
  `PrimeSpectrum.isTopologicalBasis_basic_opens` + `IsTopologicalBasis.exists_subset_of_mem_open` +
  `IsCompact.elim_finite_subcover`, index type `{p : R √ó Œ± // B p.1 ‚â§ Uf ‚äì W p.2}` carrying the cover witness,
  reindexed to `Fin t.card` via `Finset.equivFin` + `Equiv.symm_apply_apply`.
- **`IsLocalizedModule` is local on a finite spanning cover (iter-032, `isLocalizedModule_of_span_cover`, 01I8 P1b)**:
  to prove `g : M ‚Üí‚Çó[R] N` is `IsLocalizedModule (powers f)` from per-`j` localised versions over a unit-ideal
  spanning family `s : Fin n ‚Üí R` (`Ideal.span (Set.range s) = ‚ä§`), discharge the three clauses directly (no
  `of_localized_span` exists for `IsLocalizedModule` itself):
  (1) `map_units` ‚Äî `Module.End.isUnit_iff` + `Module.algebraMap_end_apply` reduces to `f`; identify the per-`r`
  localised endomorphism with mult-by-`f` via a helper (`LocalizedModule.map_mk`), then Mathlib
  `bijective_of_localized_span` (from `Mathlib.RingTheory.LocalProperties.Exactness`) gives the unit.
  (2) `surj` / (3) `exists_of_eq` ‚Äî partition of unity from `Ideal.span_pow_eq_top` +
  `Ideal.mem_span_range_iff_exists_fun`: per-cover-member extract `(s j)^a ‚Ä¢ f^k ‚Ä¢ ¬∑ = ¬∑` via
  `IsLocalizedModule.{surj,exists_of_eq,map_LocalizedModules}` + `LocalizedModule.{mk_eq,zero_mk,smul'_mk}`, BUMP
  all exponents to uniform `A,K`, then combine across the cover. The blueprint "`g_{s_j}`" is realised concretely as
  `IsLocalizedModule.map (powers (s j)) (mkLinearMap..) (mkLinearMap..) g`.
- **Affine cover-system fields (iter-029)**: (1) `faces_mem` = finite intersection of distinguished opens is

- **Affine structure theorem, conditional form (iter-029, Stacks 01HV)**: `qcoh_iso_tilde_sections` =
  `(asIso F.fromTildeŒì).symm` with `[IsIso F.fromTildeŒì]`; `moduleSpecŒìFunctor.obj F` is defeq the counit
  domain `(modulesSpecToSheaf.obj F).presheaf.obj (op ‚ä§)` so the codomain types up. Discharge the hypothesis
  via `isIso_fromTildeŒì_of_presentation F P` for a global `F.Presentation`. Mathlib provides
  `Scheme.Modules.fromTildeŒì`, `isIso_fromTildeŒì_iff`, `isIso_fromTildeŒì_of_presentation`

  never a global presentation ‚Äî that gap IS Stacks 01I8 (see Known Blockers).
- **01I8 steps (2)‚Äì(3) ‚Äî two GeneratingSections ‚üπ `IsIso fromTildeŒì` (iter-030, Stacks 01I8)**: package the
  two global generating families `œÉ : F.GeneratingSections` (epi `free œÉ.I ‚ü∂ F`) and
  `œÑ : (kernel œÉ.œÄ).GeneratingSections` into an `F.Presentation` then feed Mathlib's

  (`have P : F.Presentation := { generators := œÉ, relations := œÑ }`) ‚Äî the term-mode anonymous constructor
  defaults the `Presentation` universes to `0` and the application type-mismatches. `free` is recognised qcoh via
  `free Œπ ‚âÖ tilde (Œπ ‚Üí‚ÇÄ R)` (Mathlib `tildeFinsupp`) + iso-closure

  `qcoh_iso_tilde_sections_of_genSections`, `free_isQuasicoherent`, all axiom-clean.)
- **Cover-agnostic re-parameterization by PURE ADDITION, not delegation (iter-030)**: to generalize a Lean
  development indexed by `(ùí∞ : X.OpenCover) [Finite ùí∞.I‚ÇÄ]` to a raw finite family `{Œπ : Type u} [Finite Œπ]
  (U : Œπ ‚Üí Opens X)` when downstream files `dsimp`-unfold the originals, do NOT rewrite the `X.OpenCover` decls
  as thin wrappers `:= ‚Ä¶Fam (coverOpen ùí∞)`. A delegating wrapper unfolds only ONE layer (to `‚Ä¶Fam (coverOpen ùí∞)`),
  so a consumer's `dsimp only [cechFreeSimplicial]` no longer exposes the `Sigma.desc` structure and
  `Sigma.Œπ_desc` cannot fire ‚Äî silently breaking the downstream proof (here CechBridge:251). Instead ADD a
  parallel `section FamilyParameterized` mirroring the chain (`ùí∞.I‚ÇÄ ‚Ü¶ Œπ`, `coverOpen ùí∞ ‚Ü¶ U`,
  `coverInterOpen ùí∞ ‚Ü¶ coverInterOpenFam U`, names `‚Ü¶ ‚Ä¶Fam`), keeping every `X.OpenCover` decl byte-identical ‚Üí
  zero downstream regression. The family form subsumes the original up to defeq (`coverInterOpenFam (coverOpen ùí∞)
  œÉ` is defeq `coverInterOpen ùí∞ œÉ`), so `‚Ä¶Fam (coverOpen ùí∞)` recovers the `X.OpenCover` statement when needed.
  Use `{Œπ : Type u}` (NOT `Type`) to match `OpenCover.I‚ÇÄ : Type u`. The mechanical substitution is reuse-heavy:
  open-indexed building blocks (`freeYoneda`, `FreeCechEngine.*`, `quasiIso_of_evaluation`) carry no `ùí∞`
  dependency and are reused unchanged. (50 axiom-clean `‚Ä¶Fam` decls; `set_option linter.unusedSectionVars false`
  inside the section for combinatorial lemmas that don't use `[Finite Œπ]`, harmless ‚Äî the consumer supplies it.)
- **`‚Ä¶Fam` bridge mirror is byte-cheap when helpers are open-indexed (iter-031)**: re-parameterizing the
  CechBridge chain from `(ùí∞ : X.OpenCover)` to a raw finite family `(U : Œπ ‚Üí Opens X)` needed `‚Ä¶Fam` twins
  ONLY for the `cech*Simplicial`/`cech*Complex`-shaped decls (`homCechCosimplicialFam`, `homCechComplexFam`,
  `homCechSectionIsoAppFam`, `homCechSectionCosimplicialIsoFam`, `cechComplex_hom_identificationFam`,
  `homCechComplexMapOpIsoFam`, `sectionCechComplexMapOpIsoFam`, `injective_cech_acyclicFam`). The generic
  open-indexed/category-generic helpers (`pi_mapIso_hom_eq`, `freeYonedaHomAddEquiv_naturality`, `freeYoneda`,
  `opCoproductIsoProduct`, `piComparison`, `opFunctor`, `injective_toPresheafOfModules`,
  `quasiIso_map_preadditiveYoneda_of_injective`) apply VERBATIM ‚Äî no twin needed. Key defeq:
  `coverInterOpenFam U œÉ` is `‚®Ö k, U (œÉ k)` definitionally, exactly the shape `sectionCechComplex U F` already
  uses (it already takes a raw family), so the codomain/`Pi.mapIso` line up with NO extra `eqToHom`. The
  `injective_cech_acyclicFam` proof is the op-transport assembly of `injective_cech_acyclic` verbatim with
  substitutions, `set_option maxHeartbeats 2000000` carried (genuine nested-coercion defeq cost).
- **`Spec R` topology gotchas for cover-refinement lemmas (iter-031, `exists_finite_basicOpen_subcover`)**:
  (1) `TopologicalSpace.Opens.isBasis_iff_nbhd`'s `{U}{x}` are IMPLICIT ‚Äî apply it INLINE to the membership
  proof (`(‚Ä¶isBasis_iff_nbhd.1 ‚Ä¶) hi`), do NOT pre-bind it as a `have` (the ‚àÄ-form mismatches). (2)
  `TopologicalSpace.Opens.mem_iSup` must be applied via `.1`/`.mp` (defeq-lenient), NOT `rw`, when the
  collection is `(Spec R).Opens` ‚Äî the carrier shows as `‚Ü•(Spec R)` vs `PrimeSpectrum ‚ÜëR` and `rw` fails to
  match. (3) `(Spec R).carrier` is `rfl`-equal to `PrimeSpectrum ‚ÜëR`; `PrimeSpectrum.basicOpen g` is accepted
  directly as `(Spec R).Opens`. (4) finite span goal via `‚Üê PrimeSpectrum.iSup_basicOpen_eq_top_iff` +
  `eq_top_iff`; finite refinement of a point cover via `IsCompact.elim_finite_subcover` + `Finset.equivFin`
  reindexing + `Equiv.symm_apply_apply`.
- **Acyclic-resolution computes right-derived functor (Stacks 015E)**: the chosen comparison
  route. To identify the cohomology of the relative ƒåech complex with `R^i f_*F`, build the
  ƒåech complex as an `f_*`-acyclic resolution of `F`, then invoke one abstract lemma
  `rightDerivedIsoOfAcyclicResolution`. That lemma is built by *comparison of resolutions*:
  compare the acyclic resolution `J‚Ä¢` to an injective resolution `I‚Ä¢` of `A`
  (`isZero_rightDerived_obj_injective_succ` ‚áí `G(J‚Ä¢)‚ÜíG(I‚Ä¢)` is a `G`-quasi-iso), then transport
  via Mathlib's verified `InjectiveResolution.isoRightDerivedObj`. This replaces BOTH the
  ƒåech-to-cohomology and the Leray spectral sequences with one lemma.
- **Push-pull functoriality ‚Äî the route that ACTUALLY worked (iter-002)**: `pushPullMap_comp`
  closed by reducing `pushPullMap ‚Üí rawPushPullMap` via the `rfl`-lemma `pushPullMap_eq_raw`, then
  applying `rawPushPullMap_comp`, which states the over-triangle equalities as **free hypotheses**
  so `subst` makes every `eqToHom` transport an identity (kernel-cheap), and then uses
  `pushPull_unit_comp` + `pushPull_pentagon` (the latter wraps `pseudofunctor_associativity`). The
  proof **never touches `conjugateEquiv`**. (The `conjugateEquiv_comp` "mate-of-composite" recipe in
  `analogies/pushpull-functoriality.md` was tried first and is INFEASIBLE ‚Äî see blocker below.)
- **Syntactic object-form alignment for iso cancellation in long composites**: inside a
  `SheafOfModules` composite, `reassoc_of%`/`rw` fail when a hypothesis carries `(F ‚ãô G).obj` but
  the goal carries `G.obj (F.obj _)` (definitionally equal, not syntactic). Fix: `simp only
  [Functor.comp_obj] at h1 h2 ‚ä¢` FIRST to align object forms, THEN `reassoc_of%`. This single fix
  on `pushPull_pentagon` (iter-002) unblocked the entire push-pull functoriality cone. The lever is
  object-form alignment, not a stronger rewrite tactic.
- **Dimension shift via `Œ¥Iso`, NOT a hand-rolled LES (iter-004)**: for a short exact sequence of
  cochain complexes with an *acyclic middle* (both adjacent middle-homology objects zero), the
  connecting map is already an iso and Mathlib hands it over directly:
  `ShortComplex.ShortExact.Œ¥Iso i j hij (mid_i = 0) (mid_j = 0) : H‚Å±(X‚ÇÉ) ‚âÖ H ≤(X‚ÇÅ)`
  (`Mathlib/Algebra/Homology/HomologySequence.lean:355`). Compose with
  `InjectiveResolution.isoRightDerivedObj` on both ends to get `(R^{i}G)(Z) ‚âÖ (R^{j}G)(A)` as a
  three-step `Iso.trans` ‚Äî no `homology_exact‚ÇÅ/‚ÇÇ/‚ÇÉ` chase, which the strategy had budgeted for.
  The acyclic-middle vanishing hypotheses come from
  `isZero_homology_mapHomologicalComplex_of_isRightAcyclic` (transport `IsRightAcyclic.vanish` across
  `isoRightDerivedObj`). This is the engine `rightDerivedShiftIsoOfSplitResolutionSES`.
- **Dual Horseshoe Lemma core ‚Äî twisted-biproduct complex (iter-005)**: to build the middle complex
  `I_B` of a split SES `0 ‚Üí I_A ‚Üí I_B ‚Üí I_C ‚Üí 0` of injective resolutions, build it injective-free
  and general first. Given cochain complexes `K, L` and a cocycle family `œÑ n : L.X n ‚ü∂ K.X (n+1)`
  with `d_L^n ‚â´ œÑ(n+1) = -(œÑ n ‚â´ d_K(n+1))`, the matrix differential
  `twistedBiprodD = [[d_K, œÑ],[0, d_L]]` on `K^n ‚äû L^n` squares to zero (`twistedBiprodD_comp`,
  closed by `Preadditive.add_comp` + two `Category.assoc` + `HomologicalComplex.d_comp_d`, then
  `‚Üê Preadditive.comp_add, hœÑ, add_neg_cancel`). Assemble via `CochainComplex.of`; the
  inclusion/projection chain maps are `biprod.inl`/`biprod.snd` degreewise (built with the
  `HomologicalComplex.Hom` structure constructor + explicit `comm'`, NOT `CochainComplex.ofHom`
  which only maps between two `.of` complexes); the degreewise splitting is
  `ShortComplex.Splitting.ofHasBinaryBiproduct`, assembled to a complex-level SES by
  `shortExact_of_degreewise_splitting`. The off-diagonal `œÑ` family is an ‚Ñï-recursion carrying
  `(œÑ‚Åø, œÑ‚Åø‚Å∫¬π, cocycle)` (`twistPair`), each step `descToInjective` against
  `InjectiveResolution.exact_succ`/`exact‚ÇÄ`. (iter-005, all axiom-clean.)
- **Namespace-shadowed instance synthesis + `rw`-poisoning workarounds (iter-005)**: three recurring
  tactic hazards in the horseshoe build, all with fixes: (1) inside `namespace InjectiveResolution`,
  `Mono` of a *hypothesis* (`ses.f`) or of `I.Œπ.f n` will NOT synthesize even via `haveI`/`letI`/
  `by have` ‚Äî pass it positionally: `@Injective.factorThru _ _ _ _ _ (I.injective k) g f hMono`, and
  `(mono_of_isLimit_fork I.isLimitKernelFork)` for the resolution mono. (2) `rw [Preadditive.neg_comp]`
  silently fails on a `-x` term produced by a *prior* `rw`; `simp only [neg_comp]` makes no progress ‚Äî
  prove the equality on a FRESH `have e : ‚Ä¶ := by ‚Ä¶` goal then close with `exact e` (defeq-tolerant),
  extracted as a standalone lemma (universe metavars make `rw` erratic inside `def` bodies). (3)
  `I.Œπ.f 0` has domain `((single‚ÇÄ).obj Z).X 0` ‚Äî defeq but not *syntactically* `Z`; composing under
  another map breaks subterm matching. Wrap as `def ŒπC0 : Z ‚ü∂ I.cocomplex.X 0 := I.Œπ.f 0`.
- **Middle-term quasi-iso transfer `quasiIso_œÑ‚ÇÇ` ‚Äî built as a Mathlib supplement (iter-006)**:
  Mathlib ships only the LAST-term `quasiIso_œÑ‚ÇÉ` for a morphism `œÜ : S‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ S‚ÇÇ` of short exact
  sequences of complexes; the MIDDLE-term `œÑ‚ÇÇ` companion is an explicit Mathlib TODO. Build it by
  mirroring `quasiIso_œÑ‚ÇÉ`: for each degree `i`, `IsIso (homologyMap œÜ.œÑ‚ÇÇ i)` via
  `isIso_of_mono_of_epi` ‚Äî **epi** from `epi_of_epi_of_epi_of_mono` on the successor window
  `(Œ¥lastFunctor ‚ãô Œ¥lastFunctor).map (mapComposableArrows‚ÇÖ œÜ hS‚ÇÅ hS‚ÇÇ i j hij)` (boundary:
  `epi_homologyMap_of_epi_of_not_rel`), **mono** from `mono_of_epi_of_mono_of_mono` on the
  predecessor window (boundary: `mono_homologyMap_of_mono_of_not_rel`). Takes two boundary hyps
  `hbMono`/`hbEpi` (middle component mono/epi at a no-predecessor/no-successor boundary); for
  `ComplexShape.up ‚Ñï` only `hbMono` at degree 0 is non-vacuous. **Crucial gotcha**: discharge the
  four-lemma side-condition args (form `Epi (app' ‚Ä¶)`) with `exact hE1 i` (defeq match) ‚Äî `infer_instance`
  fails on the `app'` form; derive `Epi/Mono (homologyMap œÜ.œÑ‚ÇÅ/œÑ‚ÇÉ d)` up front from `IsIso`. This
  closed the last horseshoe leaf (`quasiIso_horseshoeŒπ` ‚Üí `ofShortExact_resolvesMiddle` ‚Üí `ofShortExact`).
- **Clean-domain ascription for `Mono (I.Œπ.f 0)` (iter-006)**: `I.Œπ.f 0` has domain
  `((single‚ÇÄ).obj Z).X 0`, defeq but not syntactically `Z`, so a `Mono` instance does NOT match a
  lemma arg typed `Œ± : S.X‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ P` (the instance pins the domain in its implicit args), and
  `[HasInjectiveResolutions ùíú]` in scope further breaks `inferInstance`. Fix: ascribe the clean
  domain in BOTH the `haveI` and the lemma argument ‚Äî
  `(show ses.X‚ÇÅ ‚ü∂ I_A.cocomplex.X 0 from I_A.Œπ.f 0)`. (Generalizes the iter-005 `ŒπC0` wrapper.)
- **`change`-to-clean-biproduct for `twistedBiprod` projections (iter-006)**: `(twistedBiprod œÑ hœÑ).X n`
  is defeq but NOT reducibly equal to `K.X n ‚äû L.X n`, so `biprod.inl`/`biprod.snd`/`biprod.lift_fst/snd`
  introduced from `twistedBiprodInl_f`/`twistedBiprodSnd_f` carry a flavour that blocks ALL `biprod.*`
  simp lemmas (even full `simp` makes no progress). Fix: `change` the goal to ascribe the clean
  biproduct `I_A.cocomplex.X 0 ‚äû I_C.cocomplex.X 0` before `biprod.hom_ext`. Also: `@[reassoc (attr := simp)]`
  registers the `_assoc` form as simp, not the bare lemma ‚Äî include the bare `biprod.lift_fst`/
  `horseshoeŒ≤_fst` explicitly when the trailing morphism is absent.
- **Left-exact functor + cycles: `mapCyclesIso` is the WRONG tool (iter-007)**: to prove
  `G(K.cycles n) ‚âÖ (G(K)).cycles n` for a left-exact (finite-limit-preserving) `G`, Mathlib's
  `ShortComplex.mapCyclesIso` is **UNUSABLE** ‚Äî it requires `[F.PreservesLeftHomologyOf S]`, i.e.
  preserve a *colimit* too, which `f_*`/left-exact `G` does not. The working route maps the kernel
  fork through `G` and re-identifies the cone point:
  `Limits.IsLimit.conePointUniqueUpToIso (Limits.isLimitForkMapOfIsLimit' G _ _ (K.cyclesIsKernel ‚Ä¶))
  ((G(K)).cyclesIsKernel ‚Ä¶)`. Compatibility with the inclusion via `conePointUniqueUpToIso_hom_comp`
  at `WalkingParallelPair.zero`. (`Functor.gCosyzygyIsoCocycles`, axiom-clean.)
- **`‚Üê G.map_comp` silently fails beside a mapped-complex term (iter-007)**: on a goal whose LHS is
  literally `G.map f ‚â´ G.map g`, `rw [‚Üê G.map_comp]` and `simp only [‚Üê Functor.map_comp]` both
  **silently fail** ("pattern not found" / "no progress") when the *rest* of the goal contains a
  mapped-complex term (`(G.mapHomologicalComplex _).obj K` ‚Ä¶) ‚Äî an instance/`HasHomology`-diamond
  reducibility quirk. Workaround: prove the `G.map _ ‚â´ G.map _ = G.map (_ ‚â´ _)` fact in an *isolated*
  `have` on a clean goal (where `rw [‚Üê G.map_comp, K.toCycles_i]` succeeds), then close the main goal
  in **term mode** (`exact hL.trans hR.symm`, using `toCycles_i` as a TERM ‚Äî `rw`/`simp` also fail on
  the mapped complex). Relatedly `rw [Category.id_comp]` fails on `ùüô (GK.X m) ‚â´ G.map f` (`GK.X m` not
  syntactically `G.obj (K.X m)`); a full `simp` closes it via defeq. (`gCosyzygyIsoCocycles_toCycles`,
  `cohomologyAppliedResolutionIso`.)
- **Epi of corestriction from exactness (iter-007)**: Mathlib has no `exactAt_iff_epi_toCycles`. To
  get `Epi (K.toCycles n (n+1))` from `K.ExactAt (n+1)`, build it via the cokernel cofork
  (`epi_of_isColimit_cofork` on the homology-cokernel data) ‚Äî NOT via the unknown constants
  `Cofork.IsColimit.epi_of_isZero_of_isColimit` / `cokernel.IsColimit.epi_of_isZero_of_isColimit`
  (both false starts this iter). (`epi_toCycles_of_exactAt`.)
- **Two-step cokernel transport beats a combined square (iter-009)**: to identify
  `coker(homologyMap(Gœà) 0) ‚âÖ coker(G.map ses.g)` when one naturality leg carries the
  `homologyMap origS.g 0` vs `(mapHC ‚ãô homologyFunctor 0).map œà` defeq, do NOT use one combined
  `cokernel.mapIso` with `p = (isoRightDerivedObj).symm ‚â™‚â´ rightDerivedZeroIsoSelf.app` ‚Äî the combined
  square forces `rw`/`cancel_epi` through that non-syntactic homology-type defeq and both fail. Instead
  split into TWO `cokernel.mapIso` steps: `coker(homologyMap(Gœà) 0) ‚âÖ coker((R‚Å∞G).map ses.g) ‚âÖ
  coker(G.map ses.g)`. Step-1 square is exactly `InjectiveResolution.isoRightDerivedObj_hom_naturality`
  (lift `ses.g` to `œà`; `comm` = `horseshoeœÜ_comm‚ÇÇ‚ÇÉ` in degree 0, extracted by `congrArg (¬∑.f 0)` +
  `simp only [HomologicalComplex.comp_f, ShortComplex.map_g, CochainComplex.single‚ÇÄ_map_f_zero]`);
  step-2 square is *literally* `(G.rightDerivedZeroIsoSelf).hom.naturality ses.g`. The `homologyMap`
  defeq is absorbed by feeding `nat1.symm` through `exact` after `Iso.comp_inv_eq`/`Iso.eq_inv_comp`,
  and the `R‚Å∞G‚âÖG` bookkeeping closes with `rw [‚Üê cancel_epi (isoRightDerivedObj G 0).hom,
  Iso.hom_inv_id_assoc]; exact (isoRightDerivedObj_hom_naturality ‚Ä¶).symm`.
  (`rightDerivedOneIsoCokerOfAcyclic`, axiom-clean.)
- **Acyclic-resolution staircase is straight-line `Nat.rec` (iter-009)**: once the leaf isos exist
  (`rightDerivedShiftIsoOfAcyclic`, `rightDerivedOneIsoCokerOfAcyclic`, `cohomologyAppliedResolutionIso`,
  `gHomologyZeroIso`, `cosyzygyShortExact`), the comparison theorem
  `(R^n G)(A) ‚âÖ H‚Åø(G K‚Ä¢)` is a generalized induction `stairGen : ‚àÄ m s, (R^{m+1}G)(cycles s) ‚âÖ
  (R¬πG)(cycles (s+m))` on `m`, with exactly TWO `eqToIso`/`omega` index bridges (`(s+1)+m` vs `s+(m+1)`,
  `0+m` vs `m`); `s+0`/`m+0`/`m+2=(m+1)+1` are defeq and need no transport. The cosyzygy middle-term
  acyclicity instance is `inferInstanceAs (G.IsRightAcyclic (K.X s))` via defeq
  `(cosyzygyShortComplex K s).X‚ÇÇ = K.X s`. (`rightDerivedIsoOfAcyclicResolution`, axiom-clean ‚Äî this
  CLOSED the P4 abstract layer.)
- **Functoriality via off-the-shelf transport (CechNerve, iter-002)**: once `pushPullFunctor` is a
  genuine functor, build the nerve by lifting the geometric backbone to `SimplicialObject (Over X)`
  (`Over.lift`), augmenting with the **terminal** `Over.mk (ùüô X)` (`Over.mkIdTerminal` ‚Äî coherence
  `w` is automatic by terminal uniqueness `.hom_ext`, no diagram chase), flipping simplicial‚Üí
  cosimplicial with `.rightOp` (NOT `.leftOp`, which un-ops the codomain; needs a type ascription),
  and whiskering through the functor via `CosimplicialObject.Augmented.whiskeringObj`, which carries
  both the structure and the augmentation.
- **Constant-coefficient combinatorial ƒåech contracting homotopy = L3 (iter-015)**: to prove
  positive-degree exactness of an alternating-coface (ƒåech) complex, model it concretely as
  `C‚Åø = (Fin n ‚Üí Œπ) ‚Üí M` with `[AddCommGroup M]`, differential
  `combDifferential t œÉ = ‚àë‚±º (-1) ≤ ‚Ä¢ t (œÉ ‚àò j.succAbove)` and homotopy
  `combHomotopy r u œÑ = u (Fin.cons r œÑ)` (prepend a fixed index `r`). Then (i) `d‚àòh+h‚àòd=id`
  (`combHomotopy_spec`): split `h(d t)` at `j=0` via `Fin.sum_univ_succ` (the `j=0` term gives `t`),
  the rest cancel termwise against `d(h t)` by `Fin.succ_succAbove_succ`-style reindexing + a sign
  flip; (ii) `d¬≤=0` (`combDifferential_comp`): a **sign-reversing involution**
  `(j,i) ‚Ü¶ (j.succAbove i, i.predAbove j)` on the double sum via `Finset.sum_involution`, using
  `Fin.succAbove_succAbove_succAbove_predAbove` (swap fixes the composite coface),
  `Fin.succAbove_succAbove_predAbove` + `Fin.predAbove_predAbove_succAbove` (it is an involution),
  `Fin.succAbove_ne` (no fixed point). Package as `Function.Exact (d) (d)` (ker‚äÜim from the homotopy,
  im‚äÜker from `d¬≤=0`) to feed `exact_of_isLocalized_span` node by node. This is the intended
  replacement for the (unavailable) simplicial `ExtraDegeneracy`. NOTE: for the localised complex the
  coefficients **vary** (`M_{s_œÉ s_r}`), so this constant version is the sign/bookkeeping *skeleton*
  that ports verbatim modulo a per-tuple family `A` + a prepend-iso `A (Fin.cons r œÑ) ‚âÉ A œÑ`.
- **`d¬≤=0` for free via `alternatingCofaceMapComplex` / `AlternatingFaceMapComplex` (iter-015)**: when
  building a ƒåech-type cochain (resp. chain) complex, do NOT hand-roll the alternating-sum `d¬≤=0`.
  Build a `CosimplicialObject` (resp. `SimplicialObject`) ‚Äî a functor out of `SimplexCategory` with
  `map_id`/`map_comp` ‚Äî and apply Mathlib's `AlgebraicTopology.alternatingCofaceMapComplex` (resp.
  `alternatingFaceMapComplex`); the differential and its nilpotence come for free. The remaining work
  is only the functor laws (a reindexing+restriction-composition proof over tuples). This is the
  pattern the relative `CechComplex` already uses (`CechHigherDirectImage.lean`).
- **Injective transfer across a right adjoint (sheaf ‚üπ presheaf of modules, iter-015)**: to show
  `(I : X.Modules) [Injective I] ‚üπ Injective ((Scheme.Modules.toPresheafOfModules X).obj I)`, feed
  `CategoryTheory.Injective.injective_of_adjoint` the sheafification adjunction
  `PresheafOfModules.sheafificationAdjunction (ùüô X.ringCatSheaf.val)` ‚Äî whose left adjoint
  `sheafification (ùüô _)` carries a Mathlib `PreservesMonomorphisms` instance, and whose right adjoint
  is `toPresheafOfModules X = SheafOfModules.forget ‚ãô restrictScalars (ùüô _)` by `rfl`. **Gotcha:** the
  one-line term form times out at typeclass synthesis because `X.Modules` and `SheafOfModules
  X.ringCatSheaf` are defeq but not the syntactically-same category instance. Fix:
  `haveI : Injective (C := SheafOfModules X.ringCatSheaf) I := ‚ÄπInjective I‚Ä∫` (it is `C :=`, not
  `X :=`); then no `maxHeartbeats` bump is needed.
- **Free‚ÄìYoneda per-term hom bijection (iter-015)**: `Hom_{PMod(O_X)}(free(yoneda V), F) ‚âÉ F(V)` is
  just `PresheafOfModules.freeHomEquiv.trans CategoryTheory.yonedaEquiv`. This is a bare `Equiv` of
  hom-sets only ‚Äî to use it in a complex iso it must be upgraded to an `AddEquiv` natural in `F`.
  Mathlib has **no** packaged coproduct/biproduct hom-equiv (`biproduct.homEquiv`, `Sigma.homEquiv`,
  `Cofan.IsColimit.homEquiv`, `coproductHomEquiv` all UNKNOWN); assemble the per-degree
  `Hom(‚®Å_œÉ AœÉ, F) ‚âÖ ‚àè_œÉ Hom(AœÉ, F)` manually from `Sigma.Œπ`/`Sigma.desc` + `Sigma.Œπ_desc`.
  *Refinement (iter-016): the `AddEquiv` upgrade `freeYonedaHomAddEquiv` is now built ‚Äî its
  `map_add'` goes via the generator formula `freeYonedaHomEquiv V F œà =
  (ConcreteCategory.hom (œà.app (op V))) (ModuleCat.freeMk (ùüô V))` + `PresheafOfModules.add_app` +
  a `change` to `ModuleCat.Hom.hom` (the term is `ConcreteCategory.hom`, defeq but not syntactic)
  then `ModuleCat.hom_add; rfl`.*
- **Dependent-coefficient combinatorial ƒåech homotopy (L3 port, iter-016)**: to get exactness of an
  alternating ƒåech complex whose coefficients *vary* per multi-index (`M_{s_œÉ}`, away localisations),
  abstract the restriction maps as additive `Œ¥ : A m (œÉ‚àòj.succAbove) ‚Üí+ A (m+1) œÉ` and prepend maps
  `c : A (m+1) (cons r œÉ) ‚Üí+ A m œÉ`, with three compatibility hypotheses: `hu` (unit `c‚àòŒ¥‚ÇÄ=id`),
  `hsh` (shift `c‚àòŒ¥_{k+1}=Œ¥_k‚àòc`), `hcomm` (coface commutation). The alternating-sum cancellation
  (`d‚àòh+h‚àòd=id`) and `d¬≤=0` (via the `(j,i)‚Ü¶(j.succAbove i, i.predAbove j)` sign-reversing involution
  + `Finset.sum_involution`) transfer verbatim from the constant-coefficient case. The only extra
  friction ‚Äî transport of a cochain value along an index-tuple equality ‚Äî is isolated to a one-line
  `depTransport` (`subst; rfl`). Live as `CombinatorialCech.Dependent.depDiff_exact : Function.Exact`,
  ready for `exact_of_isLocalized_span` per node. Gotcha: an `omit [...] in` to drop an unused
  instance variable must precede the docstring, not sit between docstring and decl.
- **Simplicial/cosimplicial object over a `Sigma`/`Pi` of representables (iter-016)**: build the
  complex by giving a hand-rolled `SimplicialObject`/`CosimplicialObject` with degree `n` =
  `‚àê` (resp. `‚àè·∂ú`) over `Fin(n+1)‚ÜíŒπ` of `freeYoneda`/`F.presheaf` on the intersection, then apply
  `AlgebraicTopology.alternating{Face,Coface}MapComplex` to get `d¬≤=0` for free (NOT hand-rolled).
  The `map_id`/`map_comp` obligations are dependent-index `Sigma.Œπ`/`Pi.œÄ` bookkeeping: close with
  `Sigma.hom_ext`/`Pi.hom_ext`; reduce by `Sigma.Œπ_desc`/`Pi.lift_œÄ`; index equality via
  `funext; simp [unop_comp, SimplexCategory.comp_toOrderHom]`; transport the injection/projection
  across it with a generic `eqToHom`-transport helper (`subst e; simp`); collapse `homOfLE = eqToHom`
  by `Subsingleton.elim` (homs in `(Opens X)`/`(Opens X)·µí·µñ` are subsingletons) + `eqToHom_map`;
  combine with `‚Üê Functor.map_comp`. Needs `[Finite ùí∞.I‚ÇÄ]` for `HasCoproductsOfShape`. For finite
  index `‚àê` (coproduct) = `‚®Å` (biproduct) ‚Äî use `‚àê`; it gives `Hom(‚àê,F)=‚àèHom` directly.
- **`PresheafOfModules.evaluation.PreservesHomology` holds by `inferInstance` (iter-016)**: homology
  of a complex of presheaves of modules is computed objectwise by sectionwise evaluation. So a
  quasi-iso / acyclicity of such a complex can be proved by exhibiting, for each open `W`, a
  sectionwise contracting homotopy ‚Äî lift objectwise via this instance.
- **Defeq-not-syntactic carrier mismatch ‚Äî the dominant tactical hazard (iter-018)**: chain/cochain
  complex carriers `K.X n` are defeq-but-not-syntactic to the underlying `K.obj (op [n])` /
  `(F.mapHomologicalComplex c).obj K).sc i` vs `(K.sc i).map F`, etc. When a `rw [hd]` substitutes a
  `.obj`-typed term into a `.X`-pinned composition, `add_comp`/`zsmul_comp`/`Œ¥_comp_aug` and friends
  silently fail to match. **Fix**: prove the underlying identity on a FRESH-elaborated standalone
  `have` (where the `‚â´` matches the helper's elaboration), then `rw`/`exact` it back. Do NOT rewrite
  into the pinned composition (re-breaks matching). (FreePresheafComplex `cechFree_d_comp_aug` repair.)
- **`‚àè·∂ú`/`op`/`Functor.map` matching needs `erw` + term-mode (iter-018)**: for products and
  contravariant-Yoneda composites, the `‚àè·∂ú` projections and `op` compositions are defeq but not
  syntactic, so plain `rw`/`simp only` silently no-op. Use `erw` for projection lemmas (`Pi.map_œÄ`,
  `piComparison_comp_œÄ_assoc`, `Pi.lift_œÄ`, `Sigma.Œπ_desc`) and term-mode `exact`/`congrArg` for
  `Functor.map_comp` combines (`‚Üê Functor.map_comp` also refuses to fire on `erw`-produced terms).
  (CechBridge `homCechSectionIsoApp_hom_œÄ`.) These proofs are version-fragile ‚Äî flag if refactored.
- **Away-localisation comparison parameterised by `Inverts`, not divisibility (iter-018)**: the
  canonical map `M_a ‚Üí Mb` between module localisations exists whenever `a` acts invertibly on `Mb`
  (`Inverts a Mb := IsUnit (algebraMap R (End R Mb) a)`), built via `IsLocalizedModule.lift`,
  characterised by uniqueness. Parameterise by `Inverts`, NOT `a ‚à£ b` ‚Äî the ƒåech prepend (`c`) map's
  source element `s r¬≤¬∑s_œÉ` does NOT divide the target `s r¬∑s_œÉ`, only its factors are invertible, so
  the divisibility form cannot type the map. `Inverts.of_dvd` / `Inverts.mul` supply the hypothesis.
  Transport-heavy dependent compatibilities (`hu`/`hsh`/`hcomm`) collapse via a bridge lemma
  (`cechCoeff_transport_eq_comparison`: `subst` + `comparison_self`) since `s_œÉ` depends only on `œÉ`.
  (CechAcyclic `AwayComparison`/`CechLocalized`, axiom-clean.)
- **HC-level homology iso from the SC-level one (iter-018)**: Mathlib has `ShortComplex.mapHomologyIso`
  but not the homological-complex-level version. Lift it: `Functor.mapHomologyIso' :=
  (K.sc i).mapHomologyIso F`, valid because `((F.mapHomologicalComplex c).obj K).sc i` is defeq to
  `(K.sc i).map F` (needs `[F.Additive] [F.PreservesHomology]`). The reusable 01XJ engine
  `PresheafOfModules.homologyIsoSheafify` (`K.homology i ‚âÖ sheafify((forget K).homology i)`) is built
  from this + `counitComplexIso` (via `sheafificationAdjunction.counit` `IsIso` +
  `isoOfComponents`); sheafification's `PreservesHomology` is `inferInstance` (exact = left-adjoint +
  finite-limit-preserving).
- **Localisation transitivity `M_a[1/b] = M_{ab}` (iter-019)**: the L1 keystone, now a project lemma
  `AwayComparison.comparison_isLocalizedModule` ‚Äî the comparison `M_a ‚Üí M_{ab}` is
  `IsLocalizedModule (powers b)`, proved via the `IsLocalizedModule.mk` constructor (surjectivity
  builds the preimage from `IsLocalizedModule.surj` of the product submonoid; injectivity via the
  helper `Inverts.smul_pow_cancel`). Powers-membership witnesses are anonymous constructors
  `‚ü®a^n, n, rfl‚ü©` against `Submonoid.powers`; the `s_r*sprod` vs `sprod*s_r` mismatch is discharged by
  `rw [mul_comm]; infer_instance`.
- **Positive-degree exactness of `D‚Ä¢ = ‚àè_œÉ M_{s_œÉ}` via `exact_of_isLocalized_span` (iter-019)**:
  `SectionCechModule.dDiff_exact`. Localise the un-localised differential at each spanning element and
  discharge each node with `map_dDiff_eq_locDiff` (`IsLocalizedModule.ext` uniqueness) +
  `locDiff_exact` (transports the localised `cechLocalized_exact`). Two non-obvious gotchas: (1) the
  per-`œÅ` `Exists.choose` index MUST be wrapped in a `private def spanIdx œÅ := œÅ.2.choose` ‚Äî inline
  `œÅ.2.choose` makes the `‚ÜëœÅ = s i` rewrite **motive ill-typed** ("motive is not type correct"); (2)
  `exact_of_isLocalized_span`'s `[‚àÄ r, IsLocalizedModule.Away ‚Üër (f r)]` are instance-implicit
  (synthesised, not goals) ‚Äî supply via `haveI inst : ‚àÄ œÅ, ‚Ä¶` BEFORE the `refine`; keep the away
  element generic in `map_dDiff_eq_locDiff` so the localised map's instance arg (which mentions `‚ÜëœÅ`)
  is never rewritten.
- **Cosimplicial/Yoneda naturality square: `erw`-everywhere + one upfront `dsimp` (iter-019)**: for
  `homCechSectionCosimplicialIso` (`NatIso.ofComponents`), plain `rw [Category.assoc]` /
  `simp only [Category.assoc]` **fail silently** ("pattern not found" / "no progress") because every
  composition's shared object is definitionally-but-not-syntactically equal (`(F.obj ‚Ä¶)` vs unfolded
  `‚àè·∂ú`/`piObj`; Yoneda hom-group carriers; `homOfLE ‚ãØ` proof-irrelevant terms). Recipe: one upfront
  `dsimp only [sectionCechCosimplicial]` to expose the product, then **`erw` for every** assoc /
  `Functor.map_comp` / naturality step, then reduce to the underlying `PMod` morphism equality and
  close with `Quiver.Hom.unop_inj` + `Limits.Sigma.Œπ_desc` + `rfl`. (Reinforces the iter-018
  defeq-carrier pattern.) Once the cosimplicial iso is built, the cochain-complex iso is a one-liner:
  `(alternatingCofaceMapComplex Ab).mapIso` of it (`cechComplex_hom_identification`).
- **Objectwise (joint-conservativity) reduction of a `PresheafOfModules` quasi-iso (iter-019)**:
  `quasiIso_of_evaluation` ‚Äî a morphism of complexes of presheaves of modules is a quasi-iso iff each
  `(evaluation R V).mapHomologicalComplex.map` is. Mathlib's single-functor
  `HomologicalComplex.quasiIso_map_iff_of_preservesHomology` is **unusable** here: it needs
  `F.ReflectsIsomorphisms`, FALSE for a single `evaluation R V` (not conservative). Build the joint
  version instead: `isIso_of_evaluation` (via `toPresheaf R` reflects isos + `NatTrans.isIso_iff_isIso_app`
  + the `rfl` defeq `((toPresheaf R).map g).app V = (forget‚ÇÇ ‚Ä¶ Ab).map (g.app V)`) +
  `isIso_Fmap_homologyMap` (`ShortComplex.mapHomologyIso_hom_naturality` + `IsIso.of_isIso_comp_left`),
  using `PreservesHomology`/`Additive` of `evaluation` (both `inferInstance`). Reusable for any
  `R : C·µí·µñ ‚•§ RingCat`.
- **Empty-case `IsZero.of_epi` needs a syntactic-image `change` (iter-020)**: to show
  `(eval V).obj (coverStructurePresheaf ùí∞)` is zero when `I‚ÇÅ(V)=‚àÖ`, the route is "epi out of a zero
  module ‚üπ target zero" (`Limits.IsZero.of_epi` + `Functor.map_epi`, eval preserves epis). The
  `Epi`/`of_epi` instance search **fails** unless the goal morphism syntactically matches the local
  `Epi` instance: `coverStructurePresheaf ùí∞` is defeq-but-not-syntactic to `Limits.image (cechFreeAug ùí∞)`
  ‚Äî `change` the goal to the `Limits.image` form FIRST (cost ~4 iterations to find). Also
  `ModuleCat.isZero_of_subsingleton` needs `Subsingleton ‚ÜëM` on the carrier, supplied via `Finsupp.ext`
  ascribed to the carrier type. (FreePresheafComplex `coverStructurePresheaf_eval_isZero_of_isEmpty`.)
- **Defeq-carrier hom-complex differential identity ‚Äî `have hop := op_sum ‚Ä¶` + `erw` + explicit `rfl`
  (iter-020)**: to prove `(homCechComplex ùí∞ F).d p (p+1) = (mapOp free complex).d p (p+1)`, reduce both
  sides to alternating (co)face sums (`CochainComplex.of_d`/`ChainComplex.of_d` with `d_squared` given
  explicitly for the `sq` arg ‚Üí `objD`), then push `op` and the additive `Hom(-,F)` through the sum.
  Plain `rw [CategoryTheory.op_sum]` and `rw [Functor.map_zsmul]` **fail "pattern not found"** though
  the goal matches verbatim (simplex notation `‚¶ãp+1‚¶å` vs `SimplexCategory.mk (p+1)` in the implicit
  source/target of the sum's `.op`). FIX: elaborate `op_sum` fresh as `have hop := ‚Ä¶` with explicit
  object args, then `erw [hop, Functor.map_sum]`; `erw [Functor.map_zsmul]` per-term; close the
  literally-identical residual with an explicit `rfl`. The complex iso is then `isoOfComponents (Iso.refl)`
  with naturality built as a TERM (`(id_comp).trans ((d_eq).symm.trans (comp_id).symm)`) ‚Äî `simp
  [id_comp, comp_id]` won't fire on the defeq-only carrier. (CechBridge `homCechComplex_d_eq`,
  `homCechComplexMapOpIso`.)
- **`(Spec R).Opens` ‚âÝ `Opens (PrimeSpectrum.Top R)` syntactically (iter-020)**: a geometric identity
  `‚®Ö‚Çñ D(s_{œÉ k}) = D(s_œÉ)` (`basicOpen_sprod`) must be **stated with the `: (Spec R).Opens` annotation**,
  else `rw` fails to match inside `tilde.toOpen`'s arguments ‚Äî the two lattice presentations are defeq
  but not syntactic. (CechAcyclic.)
- **`sectionCechComplex` is `Ab`-valued with `‚àè·∂ú` objects ‚Äî `ab_exact_iff` + `Concrete.productEquiv`,
  NOT `moduleCat_exact_iff` (iter-020)**: `sectionCechComplex` is `CochainComplex Ab ‚Ñï` whose degree-`p`
  object is the categorical product `‚àè·∂ú` in `Ab` (not a `ModuleCat` object, not a pi type), so
  `ShortComplex.moduleCat_exact_iff` does NOT apply. To turn `dDiff_exact` into `IsZero (homology p)`
  of `sectionCechComplex`, the bridge is three self-contained Mathlib-API lemmas (no new math):
  (1) `CategoryTheory.Limits.Concrete.productEquiv` (`ToType (‚àè·∂ú F) ‚âÉ ‚àÄ j, ToType (F j)`, needs
  `[PreservesLimit (Discrete.functor F) (forget Ab)]`, available for `Ab`) at element level inside
  `ab_exact_iff`; (2) unfold the `alternatingCofaceMapComplex` differential and match each
  `F.presheaf.map (restriction).op` to `dCoface` via `qcohRestriction_eq_comparison` + `basicOpen_sprod`;
  (3) `exactAt_iff_isZero_homology` + `ShortComplex.ab_exact_iff`. (CechAcyclic step (c) recipe.)
- **`Concrete.productEquiv` element-level lemmas: tactic hazards when the object is in `.obj`-form
  (iter-021, CechAcyclic step (c) BUILT)**: realising the step-(c) recipe above hit four reusable
  snags. (1) `Concrete.productEquiv_apply_apply` will neither `rw` nor `simp` against
  `ToType((sectionCechCosimplicial ‚Ä¶).obj (mk p))` ‚Äî it is defeq but NOT syntactically `ToType(‚àè·∂ú ‚Ä¶)`,
  so the family metavar `?F` cannot unify. FIX: a named term-mode restatement
  (`sectionCechProductEquiv_apply`) proved by defeq, then `rw` *that*. (2) Inlining a
  `homOfLE (le_iInf ‚Ä¶)` face-restriction term into a lemma STATEMENT triggers a `whnf` heartbeat
  blow-up (>1M, times out even at 4M with a proof). FIX: factor the term into a named `def`
  (`sectionCechFaceRestr`), keeping the dependent statement cheap. (3) `rw [AddCommGrpCat.hom_zsmul]`
  fails on `ConcreteCategory.hom (n ‚Ä¢ f)` (syntactic `ConcreteCategory.hom` vs `AddCommGrpCat.Hom.hom`)
  ‚Äî use `simp only [AddCommGrpCat.hom_zsmul, AddMonoidHom.smul_apply]`. (4) `ConcreteCategory.comp_apply`
  is `rfl` for `Ab`; use `change`/`show ‚Ä¶ from rfl` to flip `hom g (hom f x) ‚áÑ hom (f ‚â´ g) x` when
  `rw [‚Üê comp_apply]` fails on the obj-vs-‚àè·∂ú defeq. The c3 reduction
  (`sectionCech_isZero_homology_of_objD_exact`) closes via `exactAt_iff_isZero_homology` +
  `exactAt_iff'` + `ShortComplex.ab_exact_iff_function_exact`; the abstract coface match
  (`sectionCech_objD_apply`) closes via `Preadditive.sum_comp` + `ab_hom_finsetSum_apply` (Ab
  finite-sum application distributes) + `Pi.lift_œÄ` + `CosimplicialObject.Œ¥` + a final `rfl`.
- **`IsLocalizedModule.ext` over heavy `modulesSpecToSheaf` section types ‚Äî abstract the map FIRST
  (iter-022, P3 L1 tilde-bridge `phiL_naturality`)**: running `IsLocalizedModule.ext` directly over a
  concrete `modulesSpecToSheaf (~M)` section restriction `whnf`-times-out even at **2,000,000
  heartbeats** (the accessor-2 `~M` section types are defeq-intensive). FIX: `set g := (‚Ä¶restriction‚Ä¶).hom
  with hg_def; clear_value g` BEFORE `ext`, with a separate `hg` recording the only needed property
  (the `tilde.toOpen_res` `toOpen`-compatibility) ‚Äî then `ext` never `whnf`'s the heavy map. Closes at
  ~800,000 heartbeats. SECOND lesson: the resulting goal carries `‚Üë(iso).symm ‚àò‚Çó g` (a `LinearEquiv`
  coerced to `LinearMap`); `rw`/`simp [LinearMap.comp_apply / coe_comp]` and `LinearMap.comp_assoc`
  **silently fail to match** (semilinear `RingHomCompTriple` instance mismatch). Use `change`/`show` to
  the defeq fully-applied form, then `rw` the *applied* (`DFunLike.congr_fun ‚Ä¶`) versions of
  `iso_symm_comp`. The accessor-1(`Ab`)‚Üîaccessor-2(`ModuleCat`) restriction bridge (`restr_bridge`)
  must likewise be stated/`rfl`'d on an **abstract** open inclusion ‚Äî `rfl` on the concrete
  `homOfLE (le_iInf ‚Ä¶)` blows up `whnf`.
- **Engine-complex contraction ‚Üí `Function.Exact`, element extraction on `ModuleCat` homs (iter-022,
  P3b `cechEngineD_exact`)**: to package a contracting homotopy `d‚àòs+s‚àòd=id` (proved as a categorical
  hom equality `cechEnginePrepend_spec`) into a positive-degree `Function.Exact`, work element-level via
  `congrArg ModuleCat.Hom.hom (spec)` then `rw [ModuleCat.hom_add, ModuleCat.hom_comp, ModuleCat.hom_id,
  ModuleCat.hom_zero]`, then `DFunLike.congr_fun ‚Ä¶ x`, then `rw [LinearMap.add_apply, LinearMap.comp_apply,
  LinearMap.id_apply, ‚Ä¶]`. NOTE `ModuleCat.add_apply` / `ModuleCat.zero_apply` do **not** exist;
  `ModuleCat` morphisms are not directly `DFunLike` ‚Äî go through `.hom`.
- **`CategoryTheory.Limits.Sigma.whiskerEquiv` direction (iter-022)**: `Sigma.whiskerEquiv (e : Œ±‚âÉŒ≤) (w)
  : ‚àê f ‚âÖ ‚àê g` (source side reindexed), NOT `‚àê g ‚âÖ ‚àê f`. A prior analogy note had it backwards; expect
  to apply `.symm`, and pass the target family explicitly `(g := ‚Ä¶)` because higher-order unification
  fails to infer it. The chain (insertion) differential on `‚àê_{Fin(p+1)‚ÜíI} M` is the alternating sum of
  index-dropping reindexings `œÉ ‚Ü¶ œÉ‚àòFin.succAbove i` ‚Äî the chain transpose of the cochain
  `combDifferential`; this resolves the long-standing chain-vs-cochain variance question for the engine.
- **defeq-not-syntactic middle objects in the free ƒåech complex ‚Äî the 4-iter-stall escape (iter-023)**:
  the free ƒåech complex is built via `cechFreeSimplicial`/`alternatingFaceMapComplex`, whose objects carry
  index `Fin ((unop ‚¶ãp+1‚¶å).len + 1)` and degree `p+2`, **defeq but NOT syntactically equal** to the
  `Fin (p+1+1)` / degree-`p+1+1` forms from `cechFreeEval_X`/`cechEngineX`. This makes
  `rw`/`slice`/`Category.assoc`/`Preadditive.comp_sum`/`Functor.map_comp` *silently fail to match* even
  when the goal visibly contains the pattern ‚Äî the cause of the 3-iter `cechFreeEvalEngineIso` churn.
  Escapes, all used to land it: (1) **`erw [...]`** instead of `rw` (defeq matching) ‚Äî cracks
  `‚Üê Functor.map_comp`, `Category.assoc`, `Functor.map_sum`, `cechFree_d_Œπ`, `cechFreeEvalEngine_map_Œπ`;
  (2) **`refine (lemma_term).trans ?_`** instead of `rw [lemma]` ‚Äî `exact`/`refine` close up to defeq, so
  `Preadditive.comp_sum`/`comp_zsmul` go through where `rw`/`simp only` report "unused"/"not found";
  (3) **state the workhorse lemma's RHS with the clean-codomain form** ‚Äî `cechFreeEvalEngine_X_inv_hom_Œπ`
  must use `(freeYonedaEval_iso_of_le hœÉ).hom` (codomain literally `coverSectionModule V`), NOT the defeq
  `(freeYonedaAug W).app (op V)` (codomain `(eval).obj unit`), which injects a defeq middle object into
  `aug ‚â´ Sigma.Œπ` that breaks every downstream `slice`/`assoc`. Also: `HomologicalComplex.sc'_f`/`_obj_d`/
  `mapHomologicalComplex_obj_d` do NOT exist ‚Äî use `Functor.mapHomologicalComplex_obj_d`; `sc'.f`/`.g`
  reduce by `change` to `K.d`.
- **CechBridge may import CechAcyclic (iter-023)**: no cycle (CechAcyclic does not import CechBridge).
  Reuse the `sectionCech*` machinery (`sectionCechProductEquiv`, `sectionCech_objD_apply`,
  `sectionCechFaceRestr`, `sectionCech_isZero_homology_of_objD_exact`) rather than re-deriving the
  section-complex homology bridge (~100 lines saved).
- **Free-complex quasi-iso via Route-B arrow-iso transfer, NOT Homotopy repackaging (iter-024,
  `cechFreeComplex_quasiIso` CLOSED ‚Äî the 4‚Äì5-iter P3b bottleneck)**: to prove a chain-complex
  augmentation `K‚Ä¢ ‚ü∂ A[0]` is a quasi-iso, transfer from a combinatorial engine model along an
  `Arrow.isoMk'`: `quasiIso_of_arrow_mk_iso (engineAug) _ (Arrow.isoMk' _ _ chainIso rightIso hcomm)`.
  Build the four inputs: (1) **engine resolution** `engineAug_quasiIso` ‚Äî positive degrees via
  `quasiIsoAt_iff_exactAt'` + `ChainComplex.exactAt_succ_single_obj` + the prebuilt engine acyclicity;
  degree 0 via `ChainComplex.quasiIsoAt‚ÇÄ_iff` + `ShortComplex.quasiIso_iff_isIso_descOpcycles`,
  exhibiting the explicit inverse `Œπ_{const} ‚â´ pOpcycles` from a degree-0 splitting `s‚â´d+g‚â´r=ùüô`
  (`hg‚ÇÅ`/`hf‚ÇÇ`/`hg‚ÇÇ` are `rfl` ONLY against the literal `ModuleCat (X.ringCatSheaf‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî abstracting with
  `set R` defeats simp-normal form; `erw [S.p_descOpcycles]`). (2) **degree-0 evaluation bridge**
  `(eval V)(freeAug) = chainIso.f 0 ‚â´ engineAug0`, by `Sigma.hom_ext` + `by_cases V ‚â§ U_œÉ` +
  `reassoc_of%`. (3) **geometric identification** `(eval V) O_ùí∞ ‚âÖ A`: `O_ùí∞ = image(freeAug)`, eval
  preserves finite limits ‚áí `(eval)(image.Œπ)` mono, epi from the deg-0 bridge (iso ‚â´ split-epi); mono+epi
  ‚áí iso via `isIso_of_mono_of_epi` (`Balanced (ModuleCat _)`) ‚Äî feed the instance EXPLICITLY:
  `@asIso _ _ _ _ f inst`. (4) **hcomm** reduces via `ChainComplex.toSingle‚ÇÄEquiv.injective` +
  `Subtype.ext` to the deg-0 bridge modulo `singleObjXSelf` eqToHom (collapse with
  `erw [eqToHom_refl]` after `Category.assoc`). Then glue with `quasiIso_of_evaluation` + `by_cases`.
- **ƒåech-H¬π sheaf-gluing surjectivity assembly (iter-024, `ses_cech_h1` CLOSED)**: the full Stacks
  `lemma-ses-cech-h1` from a single cover with `IsZero((sectionCechComplex U F).homology 1)` + local
  lifts: form G-difference cochain (`sectionCech_objD_apply`), kill via `gœÄ` naturality (alternating
  `‚àë(-1)^i=0`), lift to F via the kernel hypothesis, extract the coboundary via the iter-023 heart
  `sectionCech_one_coboundary_of_isZero_homology`, correct the family `g' = sLoc' ‚àí fŒπ(t)`, prove
  pairwise double-overlap agreement, glue via `hGsh.isSheafUniqueGluing`, conclude by `H`-separatedness
  uniqueness. Three reusable tactic lessons (each cost real time): (a) **LSP staleness** ‚Äî
  `lean_diagnostic_messages`/`lean_goal` returned stale "no errors" after edits while `lake build` had 4;
  trust ONLY `lake env lean <file>` / `lean_run_code` mid-session. (b) `ConcreteCategory.comp_apply`
  collapse on `IsCompatible`/`IsGluing` goals needs `erw`, applied as √ók `‚Üê comp_apply` THEN √ók
  `‚Üê P.presheaf.map_comp` (NOT interleaved); parallel `Opens`-op composites then agree by proof
  irrelevance (`restr_op_unique`/`restr_inj_of_eq` via `Quiver.Hom.unop_inj (Subsingleton.elim _ _)`).
  (c) the `![i,j]‚àòŒ¥` vs `fun _=>¬∑` heterogeneous index mismatch is unsolvable by `rw`/`simp`
  (motive-not-type-correct / HEq); `restr_g'_transport` takes the tuple equality as a hypothesis and
  `subst`s it (variables ‚áí no motive issue). Also: `set_option maxHeartbeats N in` must PRECEDE the
  docstring, not sit between docstring and theorem (else `unexpected token set_option`).
- **Op-transport quasi-iso assembly for positive-degree ƒåech vanishing (iter-025,
  `injective_cech_acyclic` CLOSED ‚Äî the final P3b bridge target, first try)**: to vanish
  `(sectionCechComplex (coverOpen ùí∞) F).homology p` for `p>0` of an injective `F`, build a `QuasiIso`
  `Œò : A ‚Üí sectionCechComplex` from a degree-0-concentrated source and transfer. Steps: (1)
  `haveI : QuasiIso (cechFreeComplexAug ùí∞) := cechFreeComplex_quasiIso ùí∞` (Lane 1); (2)
  `haveI : Injective (toPresheafOfModules.obj I) := injective_toPresheafOfModules I`; (3) push through
  `(preadditiveYoneda.obj F).mapHomologicalComplex ((down ‚Ñï).symm)` applied to
  `(opFunctor _ (down ‚Ñï)).map (cechFreeComplexAug ùí∞).op`, kept `QuasiIso` by
  `quasiIso_map_preadditiveYoneda_of_injective`; (4) `Œò := œà ‚â´ (sectionCechComplexMapOpIso ùí∞ F).hom`,
  `QuasiIso` by `inferInstance` (quasi-iso ‚àò iso). Source `A = Hom(-, I)` of `op (single‚ÇÄ.obj O_ùí∞)` is
  **zero at every degree `n+1`**: `Functor.map_isZero` of `HomologicalComplex.isZero_single_obj_X`
  (note `ChainComplex.single‚ÇÄ` is *reducibly* `HomologicalComplex.single _ (down ‚Ñï) 0`, so
  `isZero_single_obj_X (down ‚Ñï) 0 _ (n+1) (Nat.succ_ne_zero n)` applies ‚Äî avoid the dead-end
  `single‚ÇÄ_obj_X_succ` / `OfNat C 0` paths), hence zero homology
  (`exactAt_iff_isZero_homology` + `exactAt_iff` + `ShortComplex.exact_of_isZero_X‚ÇÇ`). Transfer:
  `hsrcZero.of_iso (asIso (homologyMap Œò (n+1))).symm` (`IsIso (homologyMap Œò (n+1))` from
  `QuasiIsoAt` via `instIsIsoHomologyMapOfQuasiIsoAt`). Needs a **documented**
  `set_option maxHeartbeats 2000000 in` (nested `opFunctor`/`mapHomologicalComplex`/`(down ‚Ñï).symm`
  defeq coercions ‚Äî lean-auditor-confirmed legitimate, not masking). The chosen Lean form covers ONLY
  the `p>0` vanishing; the `»û‚Å∞ = I(U)` clause is a separate easy fact, left unformalized (`% NOTE:` on
  `lem:injective_cech_acyclic`).
- **Form-B absolute cohomology via `Abelian.Ext` ‚Äî four reuse-lane idioms (iter-026, `AbsoluteCohomology.lean`,
  10 decls axiom-clean)**: realizing `H^p(U,F) := Ext^p_{X.Modules}(jShriekOU U, F)` with corepresenting
  object `jShriekOU := sheafify(free(yoneda U))` (the `j_!` *functor* is absent from Mathlib; only the
  *object* is needed). (1) **`HasExt` is a `Prop` with THREE universe params** `HasExt.{w, v, u_obj}`
  (w = localized-hom universe). A bare `local instance : HasExt X.Modules := HasExt.standard _` FAILS:
  `w` auto-binds to a fresh rigid universe that won't unify with `u+1`. FIX: pin the triple ‚Äî
  `HasExt.{u + 1, u, u + 1} X.Modules` (`X.Modules` is `Category.{u, u+1}`, `HasExt.standard` yields
  `w = max v u_obj = u+1`). Make it a `local instance` so every `Ext ‚Ä¶` resolves it directly and
  dodges the `HasSmallLocalizedHom` TC-search timeout (Prop ‚áí no diamond). (2) **The category is named
  `AddCommGrpCat`, NOT `AddCommGrp`** ‚Äî `AddCommGrpCat.of (Ext ‚Ä¶)`. (3) **adjunction-`homEquiv`
  additivity via `erw [‚Ä¶]; rfl`**: to upgrade `Adjunction.homEquiv` to `‚âÉ+`, the `map_add'` goal after
  `simp only [Adjunction.homEquiv_unit]` needs `Functor.map_add` (right adjoint `forget ‚ãô
  restrictScalars` is `Additive` by `inferInstance`) + `Preadditive.comp_add`; both `rw` and `simp only`
  FAIL (defeq-carrier `Preadditive` mismatch), but **`erw [Functor.map_add, Preadditive.comp_add]; rfl`**
  closes it. `Ext.homEquiv‚ÇÄ` additivity: `AddEquiv.mk'` + `simp only [Ext.homEquiv‚ÇÄ_symm_apply,
  Ext.mk‚ÇÄ_add, Ext.mk‚ÇÄ_homEquiv‚ÇÄ_apply]` (or just use the shipped `Ext.addEquiv‚ÇÄ : Ext X Y 0 ‚âÉ+ (X ‚ü∂ Y)`).
  (4) **`Ext.comp` restatement gotchas** when writing covariant-LES wrappers around
  `Ext.covariant_sequence_exact‚ÇÅ/‚ÇÇ/‚ÇÉ`: the degree proof must be an explicit term `add_zero n` (NOT
  `by omega` ‚Äî omega can't solve `n + 0 = ?c` with `c` a metavariable), and the `‚àÉ x, x.comp ‚Ä¶ = ‚Ä¶`
  binder needs an explicit type annotation `‚àÉ x : Ext (jShriekOU U) S.X·µ¢ n, ‚Ä¶` or field notation
  `x.comp` can't resolve. Strategic payoff confirmed in-Lean: injective vanishing is the one-liner
  `Ext.eq_zero_of_injective e` because `I` is the SECOND Ext arg ‚Äî Form-A restriction-preserves-injectives
  is eliminated, not deferred.
- **New `.lean` files must be wired into the build root (iter-026)**: a freshly-scaffolded file compiles
  standalone (`lake env lean ‚Ä¶ EXIT 0`, axiom-clean) yet is invisible to the `AlgebraicJacobian.lean`
  umbrella build until `import AlgebraicJacobian.Cohomology.<File>` is added to the root. Provers cannot
  edit the root; the planner must assign the one-line import to a prover. Check `grep -rn "import ‚Ä¶<File>"`
  after any new-file lane.
- **AB4* in Ab ‚Äî product of SES is short exact (`shortExact_piMap`, iter-027)**: a product
  `Pi.map` of short exact sequences in `Ab`/`AddCommGrpCat` is short exact, but `Epi (Pi.map œÜ)` is **NOT**
  `inferInstance` (only `Mono` is). Prove the epi half elementwise: `AddCommGrpCat.epi_iff_surjective` +
  `Concrete.productEquiv` to push surjectivity through the product; exactness via
  `ShortComplex.ab_exact_iff_function_exact` (both `Function.Exact` directions are non-vacuous). This is the
  degreewise engine behind L1 of the 01EO chain (`cechComplex_shortExact_of_basis`, closed by
  `HomologicalComplex.shortExact_of_degreewise_shortExact` + this keystone).
- **Naturality of a composite `AddEquiv`, layer by layer (iter-027)**: to prove naturality of an iso built
  as `(AddEquiv from Ext.homEquiv‚ÇÄ).trans (jShriekOU_homEquiv ‚Ä¶)`, prove naturality of each layer separately
  and assemble. Key unlock: `Scheme.Modules.toPresheafOfModules X` is **definitionally** the right-adjoint
  composite `SheafOfModules.forget ‚ãô restrictScalars (ùüô _)` (verified by `rfl`), which makes
  `Adjunction.homEquiv_naturality_right` of `PresheafOfModules.sheafificationAdjunction` apply directly. The
  section carriers `F.obj (op U)` and `F.presheaf.obj (op U)` are defeq, so plain `rfl` folds them ‚Äî the
  recurring defeq-carrier `erw` obstacle did NOT bite here (`absoluteCohomologyZeroAddEquiv_naturality`).
- **Cover-local/presheaf statement form > cover-global/sheaf (iter-027)**: section-ƒåech comparison lemmas
  land cleaner stated over `U : Œπ ‚Üí Opens X` + `ShortComplex X.PresheafOfModules` + a per-face short-exactness
  hypothesis `hface`, rather than threading a cover system `(B,Cov)` and sheaf-of-modules. The geometric
  `ses_cech_h1` surjectivity enters only as `hface` at instantiation. Strictly more general, and avoids
  carrying `Cov`/`B`. CAVEAT: keep the blueprint prose in sync with the landed cover-local signature ‚Äî an
  effort-breaker sketch in the cover-global frame will mislead the prover (iter-027 lvb caught the prose lag).
- **Functor-instance synthesis through a `def` (iter-028)**: instance search does NOT see
  `PreservesZeroMorphisms` / `PreservesFiniteLimits` of a composite functor hidden behind a `def`
  (`sectionsFunctor := toPresheafOfModules ‚ãô toPresheaf ‚ãô evaluation(op V)`). Fix: `haveI : ‚Ä¶ := by
  unfold <funcDef>; infer_instance` to expose the instance before using it.
- **`ShortComplex.ShortExact` from a left-exact functor (iter-028)**: to map a `ShortExact` through a
  finite-limit-preserving functor `F`, build `hex : (S.map F).Exact` via
  `ShortComplex.Exact.map_of_mono_of_preservesKernel hS.exact F hS.mono_f inferInstance`, get
  `Mono (S.map F).f` via `inferInstanceAs (Mono (F.map S.f))` (projection-vs-application mismatch),
  `Epi` via `AddCommGrpCat.epi_iff_surjective`, then assemble with `ShortComplex.ShortExact.mk hex`.
  The anonymous `{ exact := ‚Ä¶, mono_f := ‚Ä¶, epi_g := ‚Ä¶ }` constructor is fragile here (parser + type
  mismatch). Use `change` (not `show`) for the defeq goal switch onto `S.map F`.
- **Project-`Ext` overload trap (iter-028)**: a file-local `HasExt` instance imported from another file
  lands as an *inactive* `local instance`. Without re-activation, `Ext (X.Modules object)` overloads to
  `_root_.Ext` (which expects a `Type u` argument) and then times out on `HasSmallLocalizedHom`. Fix:
  `attribute [local instance] hasExtModules` near the top of the consuming file (mirrors the
  `AbsoluteCohomology.lean` instance). This is the way to consume the Form-B absolute cohomology Ext API
  in a second file.

- **Base-ring descent of `IsLocalizedModule` (iter-041, `isLocalizedModule_powers_restrictScalars_of_algebraMap`, 01I8 Route B keystone helper)**:
  the CONVERSE of Mathlib's `IsLocalizedModule.of_restrictScalars` (which is R‚ÜíA ascent), and Mathlib LACKS it.
  Statement: for an `R`-algebra `A`, `A`-modules `M N` with `IsScalarTower R A`, and `œÜ : M ‚Üí‚Çó[A] N`, if
  `IsLocalizedModule (powers (algebraMap R A f)) œÜ` over `A` then `IsLocalizedModule (powers f) (œÜ.restrictScalars R)`
  over `R`. Proof is direct from the three `IsLocalizedModule` clauses: the only content is
  `(algebraMap R A f)^k ‚Ä¢ x = f^k ‚Ä¢ x` (`algebraMap_smul` + `map_pow`, scalar tower) and `Module.End.isUnit_iff`
  reducing `map_units` to base-independent bijectivity. This is the bridge from a tile localization (over the
  tile's base ring `R_g`) back to the global base `R` in the keystone kernel comparison.

- **`toSheaf_preservesEpimorphisms` / `toSheaf` right-exactness (iter-032; do NOT re-dispatch as a one-shot)**:
  the instance `(SheafOfModules.toSheaf X.ringCatSheaf).PreservesEpimorphisms` is the load-bearing blocker for

  package (ships only `PreservesFiniteLimits` at `Mathlib.Algebra.Category.ModuleCat.Sheaf.Limits:118`, plus

  routes verified dead in Lean: (1) `Sheaf.isLocallySurjective_iff_epi'` needs the missing
  `Epi g ‚üπ IsLocallySurjective(toSheaf g)` (and `Balanced (Sheaf ‚Ä¶ AddCommGrpCat)` fails to synthesize even
  with `backward.isDefEq.respectTransparency false`); (2) `preservesEpimorphisms_of_preserves_shortExact_right`
  needs `(toSheaf).Additive` AND `Epi(toSheaf g)` = the goal (circular); (3) stalk route = stalk-exactness of
  the SES (same fact); (4) `toSheaf ‚âÖ (forget ‚ãô toPresheaf) ‚ãô presheafToSheaf` fails because `forget`
  (= `toPresheafOfModules`) is a RIGHT adjoint, does not preserve epis. The EASY half
  `IsLocallySurjective ‚Üí Epi` IS available (`Sheaf.epi_of_isLocallySurjective`). **Next ingredient**: a dedicated
  lane building `(SheafOfModules.toSheaf R).PreservesFiniteColimits` via the sheafification adjunction (colimits
  in `SheafOfModules R` = sheafification of the `PresheafOfModules`-level colimit; coherence
  `toSheaf ‚àò sheafification ‚âÖ presheafToSheaf ‚àò toPresheaf`), several lemmas. Mathlib's analogue exists only for
  `Sheaf J (ModuleCat R)` (constant ring), not for sheaves of modules over a *sheaf* of rings. The blueprint
  `lem:to_sheaf_preserves_epi` rendered proof prose is WRONG (claims left-adjoint exactness) ‚Äî needs rewrite.

- **ƒåech L3 via `SimplicialObject.Augmented.ExtraDegeneracy` (iter-015)**: wrong variance (chain vs
  cochain) and there is no cosimplicial dual in Mathlib (confirmed `analogies/p3-localisation.md` b3).

  applies at the PRESHEAF level (no `V`-natural extra degeneracy). SECTIONWISE (fixed `V`, `I‚ÇÅ‚âÝ‚àÖ`) the
  simplicial `AugmentedCechNerve.extraDegeneracy` IS usable and is the Mathlib-blessed route ‚Äî chain

- **Building `sectionCechComplex` / `cechFreePresheafComplex` from the ƒåech nerve in `Opens X`
  (iter-015)**: `Opens X` is a poset, so the nerve's fibre products degenerate
  (`A √ó_B A = A ‚äì A = A`) and the index data `Œπ` is lost. The indexed product over `Fin(p+1) ‚Üí Œπ` is
  essential and must be constructed explicitly (cosimplicial/simplicial object on objects
  `[p] ‚Ü¶ ‚àè_{œÉ:Fin(p+1)‚ÜíŒπ} F(‚®Ö œÉ)`).
- **`Fin.val_castPred` does not exist (iter-015)** ‚Äî use `Fin.coe_castPred`.
- **ModuleCat-valued stalk route for `~` mono-preservation is DEAD (iter-033)**: to show
  `(tilde.functor R)` preserves monos one is tempted to go through `ModuleCat R`-valued stalks
  (`R`-linear by construction) and apply `IsLocalizedModule.map_injective`. This is BLOCKED: the
  Mathlib localisation handles `StructureSheaf.toStalk‚Çó'`, `stalkIso‚Çó`, `stalkToLocalization‚Çó`,
  `structurePresheafInModuleCat` (`Mathlib/AlgebraicGeometry/StructureSheaf.lean`) are all
  **module-private** (`#check` ‚Üí "Unknown identifier"); their `IsLocalizedModule` instance is
  synthesizable but the maps are not name-accessible, so `IsLocalizedModule.map`/`map_injective`
  cannot be applied against them. Use the **Ab-valued** route instead (`Scheme.Modules.toPresheaf`
  faithful/reflects-isos/preserves-limits + `app_injective_of_stalkFunctor_map_injective` +
  germ-naturality transport). Also: `modulesSpecToSheaf.ReflectsIsomorphisms` does NOT synthesize.
- **No bespoke "right-exact + preserves-monos ‚üπ left-exact" lemma is needed (iter-033)**: for
  `PreservesFiniteLimits` of an additive functor between preadditive categories with the requisite
  (co)products/zero/equalizers, Mathlib's `Functor.preservesFiniteLimits_of_preservesKernels`
  (`Mathlib/CategoryTheory/Preadditive/LeftExact.lean`) reduces the goal to "preserves every kernel
  `parallelPair f 0`". The `‚àÄ f, PreservesLimit (parallelPair f 0) F` hypothesis is consumed as a
  local instance. So the kernel route, not an image-factorisation/SES "right-exact+mono‚üπleft-exact"
  build, is the categorical glue. (Recorded because the `TildeExactness.lean` docstring wrongly
  claimed this glue is absent ‚Äî it is in-hand.)

- **P3b free `cechFreeComplex_quasiIso` ‚Äî the per-`V` contracting homotopy (iter-019)**: the
  objectwise reduction (`quasiIso_of_evaluation`) is built and reduces the named target to a SINGLE

  **Corrected ExtraDegeneracy analysis**: there is NO presheaf-level extra degeneracy (the section
  `s‚ÇÄ ‚Ü¶ prepend i_fix` is not natural across `V`, since `i_fix` depends on `V`) ‚Äî that is *why* the
  objectwise reduction is mandatory ‚Äî BUT sectionwise (fixed `V`, `I‚ÇÅ‚âÝ‚àÖ`) the extra degeneracy IS the
  clean Mathlib-blessed tool (exactly how `Rep.standardComplex.ŒµToSingle‚ÇÄ` is proved:

- **Stale `\lean{}` name ‚áí false-NEGATIVE `\leanok` (iter-005)**: the inverse of the iter-004
  code-fence trap. When a planner blueprint block names a target decl (`\lean{Foo.ofShortExact_twist}`)
  but the prover realizes the content under DIFFERENT names (a cluster: `horseshoeœÑ`,
  `horseshoeœÑ_cocycle`, `twistPair`, ‚Ä¶), `sync_leanok`'s LSP lookup of the named decl returns
  "unknown constant" and the block NEVER gets `\leanok` even though its content is complete and
  axiom-clean. Fix is the review agent's `\lean{}` correction (multi-target `\lean{A, B, C}` is
  supported, as in `lem:homology_long_exact_sequence`). Lesson for the planner: when a
  `mathlib-build` lane may abstract/rename, expect the realized names to diverge from the
  decomposition's placeholder names and re-sync `\lean{}` after the prover round.
- **`sync_leanok` / LSP code-fence trap (iter-004)**: a fenced ``` ```/`def Foo ...` signature inside
  a `/-! ... -/` doc comment is read by the `sync_leanok` declaration matcher (and `lean_file_outline`)
  as a REAL sorry-free declaration, producing a FALSE `\leanok` on the blueprint block whose `\lean{}`
  names it ‚Äî even though `lean_verify` reports "Unknown constant". This bit `lem:injective_resolution_of_ses`
  (`InjectiveResolution.ofShortExact`) in iter-004. When a strategy/handoff comment must show a
  *suggested* signature for a not-yet-built decl, write it as prose or with a `-- ` line-comment prefix,
  never inside a backtick code fence. To audit a `\leanok`, cross-check with `lean_verify <fully.qualified.name>`,
  not just `lean_local_search`/outline.
